 sikanderabad main somvaar subah ek hotel kii imaarat dhah jane se 12 logon kii maut ho gai or 14 log ghayal ho gaye
 Some people, including the son of the owner of the building, are still trapped in the rubble, whose work is on to evacuate
 police ne jaankaree di he ki sikanderabad ke raashtrapati road par sthit city lite hotel kii do manzili imaarat subah lagbhag 6
 It collapsed at 30
 police, damakal vibhaag ke karmchaaree evam bachaavkarmiyon ne malbe se 22 logon ko baahar nikaala he or inamen se 15 ko sarkari gandhi aspataal main bhartee karaayaa gaya he
 The condition of some of these injured remains critical
 kai auto-rickshaw chaalak or dihadi majdoor irani chaay or naashtaa lene ke liye yahaan maujuud the
 Andhra Pradesh Chief Minister N
 kiran kumaar reddy ne ghatnasthal kaa daura kar jaanch ke aadesh die hai
 He has asked the authorities to provide immediate relief to the injured
 isse pehle, hyderabad ke police ayukta anuraag sharma ne samvaadadaataaon ko bataaya tha ki ab tak chah shav mili hai or 11 ghayalon ko baahar nikaala gaya he
 "we are feared 20 other people may be trapped under the debris," he said
 greater hyderabad municipal corporation (jiechaemasi), damakal vibhaag ke karmchaaree, kendriya aarakshi police bal (siarpief) or hyderabad metro rail kii team malbe ko hataakar isamen fanse hue logon ko nikaalane ke kaam main juty hui he
 Rescuers have placed large cranes at the scene to remove debris
 jiechaemasi ke ayukta krishna babu is kaary kaa nirikshan kar rahe hai
 Officials said that this team has evacuated 22 people
 unhone kaha ki rashtriya aapadaa karrwai bal (andiaref) ko bhi bachaav kaary ke liye bulaayaa gaya he
 a hotel worker pulled out of the wreckage said that 30 employees were present in the building at the time of the accident
 mritkon main hotel ke chaar karmchaaree or odisha ke do log shaamil hai
 Locals have held the municipal corporation responsible for the incident
 jiechaemasi ke ayukta ne haalanki, kaha ki yah jarjar imaarat nahin thi or na hi sikanderabad kii un 57 imaaraton main shaamil he, jiske dhahaae jane ke liye notice jari kiye gaye the
 He said, the building looked stable
 imaarat ke upar bani bhatti or haleem ne shaayad imaarat ko kamjor kar di hogi, lekin vaastavik vajah kaa pataa jaanch se hi chalegaa
 The hotel owner allegedly built the furnace for the popular beef-based dish during the Muslim holy month of Ramadan
